<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="10%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;2.02.</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </B></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. is furnishing this Current Report on Form 8-K in order to furnish to the Securities and Exchange Commission a press release (the &#147;Press Release&#148;) that we will issue on
May&nbsp;17, 2011. The Press Release will disclose information regarding our results of operations for the three months ended April&nbsp;30, 2011 and our financial condition as of April&nbsp;30, 2011. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Press Release provides information regarding certain financial measures that may be considered non-GAAP financial measures (each, a
&#147;Non-GAAP Measure&#148;) under the rules of the Securities and Exchange Commission. Among those Non-GAAP Measures are: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Financial measures presented on a constant currency basis (each, a &#147;Constant Currency Measure&#148;). Constant Currency Measures are calculated by
translating the results of our Walmart International operating segment (&#147;Walmart International&#148;) for a fiscal period in the local currencies in which Walmart International operates into U.S. dollars using the currency exchange rates used
to translate the similar results of Walmart International for the prior year comparable period into U.S. dollars to report those prior period results in our consolidated financial statements. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Our total U.S. comparable store sales and the comparable club sales of our Sam&#146;s Club&#146;s operating segment (&#147;Sam&#146;s Club&#148;) for
the thirteen-week periods ended April&nbsp;29, 2011 and April&nbsp;30, 2010 calculated excluding the fuel sales of Sam&#146;s Club for such periods. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The net sales of Sam&#146;s Club for the three months ended April&nbsp;30, 2011, excluding the fuel sales of Sam&#146;s Club for that three month
period, and the percentage increase in the net sales and operating income of Sam&#146;s Club for the three months ended April&nbsp;30, 2011 over the net sales and operating income, respectively, of Sam&#146;s Club for the three-months ended
April&nbsp;30, 2010, with such net sales and operating income calculated excluding the fuel sales of Sam&#146;s Club for such periods. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Press Release provides information that reconciles each of these Non-GAAP Measures to the most directly comparable GAAP Measures. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Our management believes that presentation of the Non-GAAP Measures discussed above provides useful information to investors regarding our
financial condition and results of operations as to the periods for which they are presented for the following reasons: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We are required to translate Walmart International&#146;s operating results as stated in local currencies into U.S. dollars to report our results of
operations in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles as in effect in the United States. Period over period comparisons of our operating results can be affected by the differences between currency exchange rates in the prior fiscal
period to which the comparison is made and the currency exchange rates in the current fiscal period as reflected in our operating results reported in U.S. dollars, making an investor&#146;s assessment of the underlying performance of Walmart
International and its effect on total company underlying performance for the current fiscal period more difficult. The presentation of the Constant Currency Measures permits investors to understand important aspects of Walmart International&#146;s
underlying performance in the current fiscal period without the effect of any period to period fluctuations in applicable currency exchange rates and how that performance would have affected our results of operations in the current fiscal period and
in period over period comparisons had currency exchange rates remained constant since the comparable prior year period. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The presentation of our total U.S. comparable store sales, Sam&#146;s Club&#146;s comparable club sales, the net sales of Sam&#146;s Club and the
period over period percentage increase in the net sales and operating income of Sam&#146;s Club, calculated, in each case, excluding the fuel sales of Sam&#146;s Club, permits investors to understand the effect of such fuel sales, which are affected
by the volatility of fuel prices, on our total U.S. comparable store sales, on Sam&#146;s Club&#146;s comparable club sales and on Sam&#146;s Club&#146;s net sales and operating income for the periods presented. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:18px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="10%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Item&nbsp;9.01.</B></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Financial Statements and Exhibits. </B></FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

included herewith as Exhibit 99.1. </FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Return on investment (ROI) for the trailing 12 months ended April&nbsp;30, 2011 was 18.5 percent<FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP
STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">, compared to 19.2 percent</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP
STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> last year. The primary drivers of the change in ROI were the impact from currency exchange and cash held for pending
acquisitions. </FONT></I></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>&#149;</I></FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>During the quarter, the company returned $3.4 billion to shareholders through dividends and share repurchases. </I></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>BENTONVILLE, Ark., May&nbsp;17, 2011</B> &#151; Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. (NYSE: WMT) today reported financial results for the first quarter ended
April&nbsp;30, 2011. Net sales for the first quarter of fiscal year 2012 were $103.4 billion, an increase of 4.4 percent from $99.1 billion in the first quarter last year. Net sales for the quarter included a currency exchange rate benefit of $1.3
billion. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Income from continuing operations attributable to Walmart for the quarter was $3.4 billion, up 3.8 percent from the first quarter
last year. Diluted earnings per share from continuing operations attributable to Walmart (EPS) for the first quarter of fiscal year 2012 were $0.98, which included a benefit of $0.01 per share related to currency translation. By comparison, last
year&#146;s EPS were $0.87, which benefitted from currency translation of $0.02. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP>&nbsp;</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"></FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>See additional information at the end of this release regarding non-GAAP financial measures.</I> </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For comparative purposes, in addition to the impact of currency translation, the company had certain
discrete, pre-tax items in the first quarter of this year which are described below: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Approximately $117 million from mark-to-market gains on certain foreign currency derivative positions. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">ASDA recorded approximately a $67 million charge for the realization of expenses in the current period related to the removal of future benefit
accruals and the effect of future pay increases associated with its defined benefit plan. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Walmart Japan recorded approximately a $51 million charge for casualty losses related to the March earthquake and tsunami.
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Walmart Chile recorded approximately a $51 million gain from the sale of an investment. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All of these items are included in operating expenses, with the exception of the gain from the sale in Chile, which is recorded in membership and other
income. In summary, the net of these items accounted for approximately $0.01 of the company&#146;s EPS for the quarter. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Strong earnings
performance </U></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Walmart is reporting first quarter earnings from continuing operations of $0.98 per share, which was above
guidance,&#148; said Mike Duke, Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. president and chief executive officer. &#147;This reflects the stability and strength of our global operations. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Walmart U.S. comp sales for the first quarter were within our guidance range,&#148; Duke continued. &#147;We recognize we still have work to do and comp sales growth remains the greatest priority
for me and the entire Walmart U.S. team. The good news is that the plan Bill Simon and his team are executing is gaining traction. We&#146;re focused on delivering every day low price and a wide assortment.&#148; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Walmart International grew first quarter net sales by 11.5 percent over last year to almost $28 billion, with all countries except Japan showing sales
increases. The March&nbsp;11 earthquake and tsunami negatively affected sales in Japan. Because of the calendar shift, the majority of Easter holiday sales for International will fall in the company&#146;s second quarter. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;International remains the key growth driver for our company, and the segment is seeing continued growth through a combination of comp sales and new
stores,&#148; Duke said. &#147;Mexico, China and Chile had the highest percentage sales increases for the first quarter compared to last year.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Duke also highlighted the strong Sam&#146;s Club performance. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Sam&#146;s Club delivered
really good results this quarter, with a 4.2 percent comp that was well above our guidance,&#148; he explained. &#147;Sam&#146;s momentum is reflected in comp sales and increases in new members. The warehouse channel is increasing in importance in
the retail landscape and Sam&#146;s is gaining further momentum. We expect Sam&#146;s to add even more value to the company&#146;s overall portfolio.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">According to Duke, Walmart has tremendous growth opportunities in e-commerce. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;The recent
acquisition of Kosmix is now integrated into @Walmartlabs in Silicon Valley, and allows us to expand our capabilities in the online social commerce environment,&#148; Duke said. &#147;On Friday, we announced that we are acquiring a minority stake in
Yihaodian, one of the leading online retailers in China. We expect ongoing activity in the e-commerce area around the world.&#148; </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The company leveraged operating expenses for the first quarter. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px;padding-bottom:0px;"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Walmart ended the quarter with negative free cash flow of approximately $400 million</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">, compared to a negative $1.6 billion</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> in the previous year. ROI for the trailing 12 months ended
April&nbsp;30, 2011 was 18.5 percent, compared to 19.2 percent for the prior year. The primary drivers of the change in ROI were the impact from currency exchange and cash held for pending acquisitions. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;In March, we were pleased to report that our board declared an annual dividend of $1.46 per share for this fiscal year, a 21 percent increase over
the previous year&#146;s dividend,&#148; said Charles Holley, executive vice president and chief financial officer. &#147;We returned $3.4 billion to our shareholders during the first quarter through dividends and share repurchases. We remain
committed to returning value to shareholders.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Guidance </U></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Based on our views of the economic and sales environment in the United States and around the world, we expect second quarter fiscal 2012 diluted earnings per share from continuing operations to
range between $1.05 and $1.10, compared to last year&#146;s reported EPS of $0.97. These estimates assume that currency exchange rates remain at current levels,&#148; said Holley. &#147;We are committed to growing sales throughout all our
businesses. Leverage will continue to be a key focus, as it drives both growth and returns.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Operating Segment Details and
Analysis </U></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><U>Net sales results </U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT

quarter was above last year&#146;s first quarter. This was due primarily to sales growth, as well as expense leverage, on a flat gross margin rate. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Walmart International reported operating income that included a currency exchange rate benefit of $49 million for the first quarter. On a constant currency basis, operating income fell 3.3 percent for the

17 basis points as a percentage of sales. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Consolidated operating income for the first quarter, which includes unallocated corporate overhead,
was $5.9 billion, up 2.8 percent to last year. On a constant currency basis, consolidated operating income rose 1.9 percent to $5.8 billion. </FONT></P>

<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">%&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">During the 13-week period, the majority of
the Walmart U.S. comparable store sales decrease was due to a decline in traffic, while average ticket was up versus the prior year. Grocery and health and wellness categories had positive comp sales for the first quarter. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For the 4-5-4 period from April&nbsp;30 through July&nbsp;29, 2011, Walmart U.S. expects comparable store sales to range from negative one percent to
positive one percent. The Walmart U.S. 13-week comp for the second quarter of fiscal 2011 declined 1.8 percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;We are monitoring the
economic environment carefully, as significant changes in gas prices and inflation during the quarter will influence our actual performance,&#148; said Bill Simon, Walmart U.S. president and chief executive officer. &#147;We continue to focus on
delivering EDLP across the store.&#148; </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">4 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For Sam&#146;s Club, comparable ticket, excluding fuel, increased for both Business and Advantage members
for the 13-week period. Comparable traffic, excluding fuel, increased for Advantage members and was relatively flat for Business members. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Sam&#146;s Club expects comp sales, without fuel, for the current 13-week period, to increase between three percent and five percent. Last year,
Sam&#146;s Club comp, without fuel, for the second quarter comparable 13-week period rose 1.0 percent. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Our second quarter is under way
and we expect our strong sales momentum to continue across grocery, home and apparel,&#148; said Brian Cornell, Sam&#146;s Club president and chief executive officer. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Both Walmart U.S. and Sam&#146;s Club will report comparable sales for the 13-week period on Aug. 16, when the company reports second quarter results. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Notes </U></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Constant currency results
are calculated by translating current year results using prior year exchange rates. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">After this earnings release has been furnished to the
Securities and Exchange Commission (SEC), a pre-recorded call offering additional comments on the quarter will be available to all investors. Callers may listen to this call by dialing 800-778-6902, or 585-219-6420 outside the U.S. and Canada.
Information included in this release, including reconciliations, and the pre-recorded phone call are available in the investor information area on the company&#146;s website at www.walmartstores.com/investors. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. (NYSE: WMT) serves customers and members more than 200&nbsp;million times per week at 9,029 retail units under 60 different banners
in 15 countries. With fiscal year 2011 sales of $419 billion, Walmart employs more than 2&nbsp;million associates worldwide. Walmart continues to be a leader in sustainability, corporate philanthropy and employment opportunity. Additional
information about Walmart can be found by visiting http://www.walmartstores.com. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Forward Looking Statements </U></B></FONT></P>

segment of the company for the 13-week period from Apr. 30, 2011 through Jul. 29, 2011, and management&#146;s expectations that the company&#146;s Sam&#146;s Club segment&#146;s momentum will lead to even more value from that segment to the

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">9 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Reconciliations of and Other Information regarding Non-GAAP Financial Measures </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(Unaudited) </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>(In millions, except per share data) </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The following information provides reconciliations of non-GAAP financial measures presented in the press release to which this reconciliation is attached to the most nearly comparable financial measures
calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;). The company has provided the non-GAAP financial information presented in the press release, which is not calculated or presented in accordance
with GAAP, as information supplemental and in addition to the financial measures presented in the press release that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. Such non-GAAP financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a
substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. The non-GAAP financial measures in the press release may differ from similar measures used by other
companies. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Free Cash Flow </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We define free cash flow as net cash provided by operating activities in a period minus payments for property and equipment made in that period. Negative
free cash flow was approximately $400 million and $1.6 billion for the quarters ended April&nbsp;30, 2011 and 2010, respectively. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Free cash
flow is considered a non-GAAP financial measure under the SEC&#146;s rules. Management believes, however, that free cash flow, which measures our ability to generate additional cash from our business operations, is an important financial measure for
use in evaluating the company&#146;s financial performance. Free cash flow should be considered in addition to, rather than as a substitute for, income from continuing operations as a measure of our performance and net cash provided by operating
activities as a measure of our liquidity. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Additionally, our definition of free cash flow is limited, in that it does not represent residual
cash flows available for discretionary expenditures due to the fact that the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual obligations or payments made for business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is
important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Although other
companies report their free cash flow, numerous methods may exist for calculating a company&#146;s free cash flow. As a result, the method used by our management to calculate free cash flow may differ from the methods other companies use to
calculate their free cash flow. We urge you to understand the methods used by another company to calculate its free cash flow before comparing our free cash flow to that of such other company. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The following table sets forth a reconciliation of free cash flow, a non-GAAP financial measure, to net cash provided by operating activities, a GAAP
measure, which we believe to be the GAAP financial measure most directly comparable to free cash flow, for the quarters ended April&nbsp;30, 2011 and 2010, as well as information regarding net cash used in investing activities and net cash provided
by financing activities in those periods. </FONT></P>

<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Calculation of Return on
Investment and Return on Assets </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Management believes return on investment (&#147;ROI&#148;) is a meaningful metric to share with investors
because it helps investors assess how effectively Walmart is employing its assets. Trends in ROI can fluctuate over time as management balances long-term potential strategic initiatives with any possible short-term impacts. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">ROI was 18.5 percent and 19.2 percent for the trailing 12 months ended April&nbsp;30, 2011 and 2010, respectively. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">We define ROI as adjusted operating income (operating income plus interest income, depreciation and amortization, and rent expense) for the fiscal year
or trailing twelve months divided by average invested capital during that period. We consider average invested capital to be the average of our beginning and ending total assets of continuing operations plus accumulated depreciation and amortization
less accounts payable and accrued liabilities for that period, plus a rent factor equal to the rent for the fiscal year or trailing twelve months multiplied by a factor of eight. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">ROI is considered a non-GAAP financial measure under the SEC&#146;s rules. We consider return on assets (&#147;ROA&#148;) to be the financial measure computed in accordance with GAAP that is the most
directly comparable financial measure to ROI as we calculate that financial measure. ROI differs from ROA (which is income from continuing operations for the fiscal year or trailing twelve months divided by average total assets of continuing
operations for the period) because ROI: adjusts operating income to exclude certain expense items and adds interest income; adjusts total assets from continuing operations for the impact of accumulated depreciation and amortization, accounts payable
and accrued liabilities; and incorporates a factor of rent to arrive at total invested capital. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Although ROI is a standard financial metric,
numerous methods exist for calculating a company&#146;s ROI. As a result, the method used by Walmart&#146;s management to calculate ROI may differ from the methods other companies use to calculate their ROI. We urge you to understand the methods
used by another company to calculate its ROI before comparing our ROI to that of such other company. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">11 </FONT></P>



<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

financial measurement, is as follows: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Wal-Mart Stores, Inc. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Return on Investment and Return on Assets </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
